as[\s\-\–]malvinas\b|\bfalklandseyjar\b|\b[iìîíïīǐ]les[\s\-\–]malouines\b|\bfalklandsullot\b|\bෆෝක්ලන්ත[\s\-\–]දූපත්\b|\billas[\s\-\–]malvinas\b|\bfɔlkman[\s\-\–]aeland\b|\bfalklandinseln\b|\binizi[\s\-\–]falkland\b|\bफकल्याण्ड[\s\-\–]टापु\b|\bfalklandsøyene\b|\bfalklands[oôóòöō]arna\b|\billes[\s\-\–]malvines\b|\bfalklandsøerne\b|\bfalklandsøyane\b|\bilhas[\s\-\–]malvinas\b|\b[iìîíïīǐ]les[\s\-\–]falkland\b|\bν[ηή]σοι[\s\-\–]φ[ωώ]κλαντ\b|\bجزایر[\s\-\–]فالکلند\b|\bmaluwini[\s\-\–]gun\b|\bnosy[\s\-\–]falkand\b|\bየፎልክላንድ[\s\-\–]ደሴቶች\b|\bجزر[\s\-\–]فوكلاند\b|\bफॉकलंड[\s\-\–]बेटे\b|\bאיי[\s\-\–]פוקלנד\b|\bフォークランド諸島\b|\bfalklandy\b|\bfalklandi\b|\bmalvinak\b|\b포클랜드[\s\-\–]제도\b|\b福克兰群岛)\b
